Its been about 9 years ago that i took Scott my 1999 yz250 engine for a rebuild. It turns out that the casing had a crack where the oildrain plug is at and it was leaking oil, and so they told me about it and offered to weld the crack to repair it but that the oil changes will be done from the clutch cover. I accepted the idea. They told me that the original crank was still good so i kept it to keep the cost low. The motor had the bearings and all seals replaced and we went with a vertex cast piston. I've ridden this dirtbike almost every weekend for about 3 hours per ride for the past 9 years ever since, and never has anything failed on it. Compression has always been good and i replaced the top end myself just because i wanted to inspect the piston (because 2-stroke) 3yrs ago and i went again with Vertex. The top-end was still good but replaced it anyway since i had already taken it apart. Needless to say, the guys' craftsmanship experience have stood the test of time on this example here at R tillery. I always bring my bikes here when i have an issue i can't solve and they never dissapoint. Thank you Scott and your team for the quality service.< /Text>

<date>1545802871397<//date><Rating>2<//Rating>< Text>
Perhaps it's not our taste, but we did not enjoy most of our food. We ordered 8 different skewers. All of them were coated in heavy cumin seasoning. The cumin was very strong and overpowering, while the marinade was weak. I don't know if it's authentic Chinese, but lamb, corn cobs, chicken gristle: it was all one seasoning.
We also got a "Pork & Tofu Casserole," which was a flavorful soup with glass noodles (albeit very few noodles).
The prices are a bit high, considering the adjacent restaurants in the same lot serve tastier food and charge less.
I would not recommend this place, but if the heavy-handed cumin seasoning sounds appealing to you, this might be the place for you.< /Text>

<date>1621393255769< /date><Text>I was offered a couple of nights lodging at the UCLA Meyer and Renee Luskin Conference Center. When David, with the inside-scoop mentioned that it was 'Swank', I of course decided to give it a try. Google maps directed me into the loading dock at first, until I was able to discover the Guest Parking, located beneath the building,  accessible via a down-ramp that is adjacent to the guest drop-off / pick-up zone loop. The lobby is modern, warm, spacious with paneled details interspersed and appointed with gracious textures. The lobby has several work station areas available for guests. I was warmly greeted by the front desk staff, with comprehensive health safety protocols. The room was easily accessible from the security room-key enabled elevators. Echoing the modern motif, the room was tidy, with entry table, wardobe (with safe), integrated dresser, counter, desk & work chair, and large HDTV along the long wall, a comfortable reading chair, and king sized bed with side tables,  opposite. Numerous and well placed light fixtures facilitated getting comfortable. The bathroom is spacious with large lovely border-lit mirror and walk-in shower. The room was quite quiet :-) ...Thanks so very much for the ample hospitality and attention to detail...Thanks David, all of my 'Swank'  expectations have been exceeded!< /Text>< resp>

< Review>
We went here yesterday for our son's eleventh birthday. The exhibits are truly amazing. The rainforest dome, the albino aligator and the penguins were my favorites, not to mention the gorgeous 'Living Roof.' The food in the cafeteria is a bit pricey, but tastes incredible. My artichoke and wheatberry salad was excellent. The entire staff is also super friendly and eager to answer any questions you may have about the exhibits. My only complaint would have to be the fact that this place is expensive as heck. After the cost of admission and a meal at the cafeteria, a family of four can easily spend over three hundred bucks. All in all though, a great experience...just expect to be charged an arm and a leg.<//Review>

Really upscale and nice place!! Lots of amenities for guests and the staff is all super nice (and there is a no tipping policy throughout the hotel including valet, restaurant, and bar). My only complaint was that there is a charge if you'd like a mini fridge and I did not find this out until checkout. You'd think a place this nice would offer one for free, but even if they're going to charge, I wish they made it more clear. Other than that, a truly wonderful stay! A legendary property that I would absolutely return to.</review>

This hotel is nice, clean, and well run. Rooms are immaculate and facilities are nice. There's a restaurant attached to it, with reasonably priced food. The elevator was hard to figure out for many guests. You have to hold your key card on a sensor below the floor numbers and wait for the light to turn green.
